Current Commentary

Reflections on the US's Further Increase in Silver Prices 18

— Yan

According to a US telegram on the 10th, President Roosevelt has decided to increase the price of buying domestically produced silver from 64.5 cents per ounce to 71 cents, effective from today. Since the announcement of this news, the world's silver problem has responded accordingly and has seen obvious new developments. The price increase trend started with New York's benchmark price rising from 65.75 cents to 66 cents. In London, on the 11th, the benchmark silver price for immediate delivery rose from 28.9375 pence to 29.6875 pence, and the price for forward delivery rose from 29.0625 pence to 29.8125 pence, creating a nine-year high. In the afternoon, due to US purchases, the silver price rose another 0.25 pence, with the current price at 29.9375 pence and the price for forward delivery at 30.0625 pence. In Japan, the price will be raised by 1.80 yuan to 71.764 yuan.

Since the world's silver market has risen along with the US's further increase in domestic silver prices, looking back at the situation in our country, although the exchange rate has plummeted as a result, the changes in foreign exchange have been very weak, and the balancing tax rate remains at 6.75%. This abnormal phenomenon is puzzling to our people. According to experts, if the recent London silver price is compared with our country's exchange rate against the pound sterling, the difference is about 3.10%. The highest difference last autumn was only 20%. If silver is exported at this time, after deducting all expenses such as export tax, balancing tax, freight, and insurance, the net profit is estimated to be about 11-12%. That is, for every 1 million yuan of silver exported, the net profit is 110,000-120,000 yuan. Compared with last year's net profit of 6-7%, the excellent profit is probably beyond anyone's initial expectations. From this point of view, if our country's silver reserves are not prevented in advance, there will be a continuing trend of reduction.

Furthermore, according to the US silver purchase plan, the silver that needs to be purchased should be based on the existing gold reserves of 8,599,743,000 yuan. Based on the ratio of gold to silver as 3:1, the treasury should have silver reserves worth 2,866,580,000 yuan. However, according to a check, the current silver reserves of the US Treasury are only worth 915,614,000 yuan, which is less than one-third of the set amount. If the Americans insist on their established policy and continue to buy silver, they may end up including our China and India's silver reserves, which may still be insufficient. Our country's monetary system will suffer unprecedented sacrifices in history. It can be said that the US's implementation of a further increase in silver prices has been going on for two days, and our government authorities seem to be still waiting for the development of events. We have not yet heard what countermeasures will be taken. Even the balancing tax rate has not been raised accordingly. In my humble opinion, under this serious situation, effective measures to prevent the continued export of silver reserves must be taken decisively and formulated as soon as possible. If the delay continues, the impact may be far greater than in the past.

Aiming to Guarantee Peace: Britain, France, and Italy Maintain Unity; British Representative Expresses Sincere Desire to Help Advance Group Security 19

Stresa – The leading figures of the three major European powers commenced a meeting here yesterday to discuss various issues related to pacifying Europe. It was firmly declared during yesterday's meeting that regarding France's appeal to the League of Nations concerning Germany's military buildup, the fact that France, Italy, and Britain have jointly presented this matter to the League is no longer in question. The French appeal to the League is solely for French documentation purposes and will not be altered in the meeting.

British Representative Issues Declaration – British representatives MacDonald and Simon yesterday explained to the French and Italian representatives the UK's stance on peace and security issues in detail, expressing Britain's willingness to assist in advancing the European group security system through various practical methods.

A Reuters reporter learned that the British representative issued a declaration stating that the UK is willing to do everything in its power to consolidate the unity agreed upon between Britain, France, and Italy. The British representative declared that no country should feel it is overstepping its bounds for the sake of its own policies. Britain, France, and Italy cannot be separated on matters that can strengthen European peace. The British representative also stated that the British government is currently preparing a disarmament plan and is willing to have it supervised by the League of Nations. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(London) According to a special correspondent for the Times, British Prime Minister MacDonald made a declaration at the first Stresa meeting yesterday, with the catchphrase, "Britain, France, and Italy share the common goal of safeguarding European peace. It is inconceivable that the three countries would allow themselves to be divided in this endeavor. According to British policy, the League of Nations is the appropriate forum for international negotiations to maintain peace. Britain is prepared to make a substantial contribution to promote collective security." (National Telegram, 12th)

Second Day of the Meeting – Stresa – The meeting of Britain, France, and Italy continued this morning at 9:30 AM and concluded at 11:00 AM. The discussions this morning concerned the consequences that might arise from France's application to the League of Nations Council, and the appropriate steps to be taken in the future in the event of further breaches of treaties. After the meeting, a reporter interviewed British Prime Minister MacDonald, asking whether the reported British policy from London was accurate. MacDonald replied, "You should know that the qualified representatives of the British government are present here." (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Stresa – When the representatives of Britain, France, and Italy gathered this morning, the primary subject of discussion was the unilateral denial of international obligations. It is heard that the scope of the discussion was quite broad, not solely focused on Germany. Consideration of the French appeal to the League of Nations has been completed, and the recommendations contained in the London communiqué of February 3 will now be studied in detail (i.e., Britain and France both agree on the necessity of maintaining Austria's independence and integrity, and advocate inviting Germany to genuinely cooperate; Britain and France do not regard the unilateral denial of international obligations as right, welcome the conclusion of a European mutual assistance pact, and suggest replacing the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles with an agreement, Germany returning to the League of Nations, and the conclusion of an air pact). The afternoon meeting is scheduled to begin at 2:30 PM. In addition to the London communiqué, the agenda also includes Eastern European and Central European pacts. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Hoping Germany Returns to the League of Nations – Stresa – The representatives of Britain, France, and Italy held their second meeting at the Palazzo Borromeo at 9:30 AM this morning. It is heard that they will thoroughly discuss Italy's views. Yesterday, the press and the representatives in attendance discussed the British delegation's memorandum, which was far richer in content than the opinions of other countries. Its conclusion stated that the main purpose of Britain's participation in the Stresa conference is to promote Germany's return to the League of Nations. However, Prime Minister MacDonald also stated that inviting Germany to participate in the Stresa conference at this time would be unwise. This declaration is tantamount to an informal denial of the suggestion to invite Germany, Poland, and Soviet Russia to a six-nation conference. Summarizing the news before today's meeting, all three countries seem to hope that Germany will return to the League of Nations, but Britain has expressed this more clearly than Italy and France. (National Telegram, 12th) Although there are various rumors circulating regarding the Stresa conference, it is confirmed that yesterday's meeting focused on the following three items:

(1) The possibility of Germany's return to the League of Nations; (2) The independence of Austria; (3) To ensure that the clauses of the League of Nations Covenant regarding dealing with aggressors are implemented promptly when relevant situations arise, thereby strengthening the Covenant. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Main Topics of Discussion the Day Before – The majority of the time during yesterday's meeting was spent on France's appeal to the League of Nations, and this led to the issue of Germany's return to the League of Nations being mentioned. The British side believes that this should not be conditional, as imposing conditions may be unhelpful and even harmful.

The issue of an Eastern European pact, along with France and Russia's recent understanding, was also thoroughly studied. It is heard that the possibility of Germany joining this pact was not discussed.

Friendly Atmosphere of the Talks – Yesterday afternoon's discussion lasted for two and a half hours. According to Italian sources, the atmosphere was very friendly. The general sentiment among the British here is that the meeting has made a good start, and there are no differences of opinion among the three countries in principle. The meeting may have to be extended to Saturday or Sunday, which is seen here as a sign that the discussions have revealed something of definite value. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Basic Policy Towards Germany – The Three Countries Agree – Stresa – It was learned today that Britain, France, and Italy have agreed not to allow any event to hinder the joint action of the three countries towards Germany. The three countries feel that if there are any differences of opinion on basic policy, they will fall into Germany's trap. Therefore, there will be no modification to the document that France sent to the League of Nations requesting a thorough discussion of Germany's abandonment of the Treaty of Versailles. Furthermore, it has been learned from reliable sources that Germany, Poland, and Soviet Russia will also be invited to send representatives to attend the meeting here, and the current talks will be a preparatory meeting. It is heard that Britain has managed to prevent France and Italy from taking drastic measures against Germany this morning.

Communique Issued After the Meeting – The Italian government issued a communiqué last night, reporting on the situation of the first meeting, stating only that, "British Prime Minister MacDonald briefly outlined Britain's foreign policy this morning. Afterwards, British Foreign Secretary Simon reported on his tour of Europe and described Germany's attitude towards the Danube Pact, the Eastern European Pact, the Air Defense Mutual Assistance Pact, and the League of Nations. In the afternoon meeting, the French representative explained the reasons for his report to the League of Nations and presented the plans he hoped to take."

Reasons for France's Appeal to the League of Nations – The three-country meeting opened at 10:30 AM yesterday morning. The French representative first presented France's document to the League of Nations. The document, which is likely to be released on Monday, is very pessimistic in tone. Although it does not predict war, it emphasizes the seriousness of the crisis and believes that it can still be resolved if efforts are made. The document was submitted by French Foreign Minister Laval to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Prime Minister MacDonald, but was not requested for their approval, and therefore is purely a French plan that does not require the consent of other countries. However, Laval also stated that he very much wanted other countries to know the reasons stated in the document, because if other countries followed Germany's actions, the results would be unimaginable. Subsequently, Foreign Secretary Simon spoke about the results of his tour of various countries' capitals and answered the questions of Mussolini, Laval, and French Prime Minister Flandin. The French representative continued, saying that their impression of the meeting was very good.

Points Demanded by Italy and France – Afterwards, the representatives of the three countries discussed the French document in detail and learned that France and Italy had asked Britain to restrain Germany. The plans of France and Italy include the following points:

(1) France demands that if Germany violates the Treaty of Versailles again, it should be punished.

(2) France and Italy insist that the demilitarization of the Rhineland and the independence of Austria must not be violated.

(3) France and Italy demand that the scope of the Locarno Treaty be expanded, with the addition of a Danube Treaty, including countries such as Czechoslovakia, Romania, Yugoslavia, Austria, and Hungary.

(4) France demands that the League of Nations Council condemn Germany's violation of the treaty. (National Telegram, 12th)

Statement from the British Government

(London) Officials fear that the outside world will have the wrong impression of the opinions expressed by the British representative in Stresa yesterday, so they stated today that since the British representative set off for Stresa, Britain has not made any new decisions or issued any formal new announcements. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

British Policies Are Generally Summarized into Five Points 20

(Paris) According to a special correspondent for this agency in Stresa, the ministers of Britain, France, and Italy held a meeting this morning, most of the time was spent by the British representative presenting a report on the proposal to invite Germany, Russia, Poland, and Czechoslovakia. Foreign Secretary Simon also explained the purpose of this trip, which was to study whether Germany can still cooperate in the cause of European peace. As for Britain's attitude towards this meeting, it is nothing more than the following: (1) The countries participating in the meeting have an obligation to show a relationship of solidarity, and Britain is prepared to do everything in its power to show that spirit of solidarity; (2) Within the scope of the League of Nations, a collective security system should be organized, and Britain is willing to support it with real strength in various practical forms; (3) The cause of peace must be organized, and the method of organization is to determine and supervise the ratio of each country's armaments; (4) Britain is still willing to respect the Rome Four-Power Pact of July 15, 1933, but in the current situation, the relationship of solidarity between Britain, France, and Italy, and the power of the League of Nations should be taken as the basis for action; (5) Britain wishes Germany to return to the League of Nations, but in the current situation, it is not appropriate to allow it to rejoin unconditionally, so as not to create an extremely bad precedent. At this point, French Foreign Minister Laval explained France's application to the League of Nations for Germany's rearmament. It is heard that Britain and Italy will definitely support it in the future. It is rumored that after the end of the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Council on the 15th of this month, a meeting will be held again in Stresa, and Germany will be invited to participate. This statement has been denied by French officials. (Havas dispatch, 11th)

British Prime Minister Will Not Go to Geneva 21

(London) Yesterday's telegram stated that Prime Minister MacDonald, after attending the Stresa conference, planned to go to Geneva to attend the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Council to be held on the 15th. According to the Daily Mail's diplomatic correspondent in Stresa, the Prime Minister has decided not to go to Geneva. The Daily News reporter believes that the British delegation to the Stresa meeting is now insisting that Germany must participate in any international conference held after the end of the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Council. The Daily Herald also believes that although Germany is currently refusing to participate in the mutual assistance pact, the British cabinet believes that the country will definitely reconsider this attitude. The newspaper also said that Britain will continue to work hard to persuade Germany to comply and explore the true purpose of German policy. In addition, The Times mentioned an article published in the Italian newspaper Il Popolo d'Italia yesterday, stating that it is not impossible to convene a second international conference and conclude a six-nation pact between Britain, France, Italy, Russia, Germany, and Poland. (According to an article published in the Italian newspaper Il Popolo d'Italia yesterday, it stated that in the near future, it is possible to invite Russia, Germany, and Poland to hold another international conference with Britain, France, and Italy.) It also said that France's wish is to fully clarify what measures should be taken to deal with Germany if it violates the Treaty of Versailles again and what their nature should be. In other words, it would be in accordance with the League of Nations regulations on page 9.

Expanding the Scope of the Conference: Inviting Germany, Poland, and Russia to Participate; British-Italian Understanding May Be Realized; The Meeting Place Will Be in London, the British Capital 22

Stresa – Well-informed circles today commented on Italy's opinion that there may be a larger international conference in the near future, in which Germany, Poland, and Soviet Russia will be invited to participate, saying that this is only music in the air, and pleasant music at that. Although all Italian newspapers this morning regarded any concrete decision on this matter as wishful thinking, according to a Reuters diplomatic correspondent, all parties in Stresa feel that this kind of meeting may soon be realized, and the meeting place may be in London, especially because Italy and Britain have apparently had a close understanding in the last 24 hours. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

Rome – After the commentary written by Il Popolo d'Italia on Thursday was published, all the evening newspapers reprinted it. According to the Fascist newspaper Il Tevere, it is still doubtful whether Germany, Poland, and Soviet Russia will be invited to participate in the Stresa conference. Although France has expressed opposition to Germany, Britain still has considerable influence. As for what Italian Prime Minister Mussolini said, Italy now has 600,000 soldiers wielding weapons and the latest weapons, which is enough to express Italy's position. Therefore, Italy can wait calmly for any changes in the international situation without fear. (National Telegram, 12th)

The implementation of economic and financial sanctions stipulated in Article 16 of the Covenant is particularly important. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

Supporting the Conclusion of a Security Pact 23

(London) According to information obtained from responsible sources, the British cabinet now supports the conclusion of a pact similar to the French-Russian agreement, and believes that this kind of pact is a good foundation for a collective security organization. However, before the final decision is made to conclude this kind of pact, Britain must understand whether Germany is truly willing to participate in the collective security system. If, after various efforts, Britain is still unable to get Germany to participate in the security system, then Britain will not oppose the conclusion of an agreement to protect the security of the countries concerned. In addition, responsible sources solemnly stated that Britain, in any case, does not want to be subject to any new constraints on the European continent, but Britain will definitely support the Locarno Treaty and the mutual assistance pact proposed in the London Declaration of February 7. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

France Takes a Tough Stance: Plans to Use the League of Nations Covenant to Restrain Germany 24

Stresa – An Associated Press reporter learned that France will insist within the League of Nations on sanctioning Germany's unilateral actions in violating the treaty, and will demand the stipulation of several kinds of sanctions. French Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval are currently studying these sanction measures, but it is heard that these sanctions may not be military in nature, but rather an economic sanction that League of Nations member states can unanimously impose on Germany, according to the provisions of Article 16 of the Covenant. (National Telegram, 11th)

(Paris) French reporters now believe that French Prime Minister Flandin will take a tough stance against Germany at the Stresa conference. Le Matin now believes that the French representative will ask for a formal declaration that Germany has violated the treaty. Flandin intends to suggest that a common attitude be taken in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant. If Germany continues to violate the Treaty of Versailles, Britain, France, and Italy should impose financial and economic sanctions on Germany. A reporter for Paris-Soir claims that the French and Italian representatives have already agreed on this course of action at the Stresa conference. According to the French account of the situation at the Stresa meeting today, French Foreign Minister Laval explained the reasons why France requested that the League of Nations Council convene a meeting because of Germany's decision to implement compulsory military service. It is said that the League of Nations Council's approval of the resolution endorsing France's appeal, without explicitly mentioning Germany or imposing any sanctions on Germany, is sufficient as a moral condemnation to be imposed on Germany. Because the general public was quite optimistic about the Stresa conference, the price of government bonds suddenly rebounded on the stock exchange today. (Reuters dispatch, 12th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat received an informal notice today, "stating that Poland is unwilling to participate if the League of Nations Council passes a resolution condemning Germany at its meeting on April 15." (National Telegram, 11th)

Optimistic Tone in Paris Newspapers 25

(Paris) After the first day of work at the Stresa conference, all the newspapers expressed optimism about the future of the conference, believing that the solidarity between Britain, France, and Italy has been effectively demonstrated, and British Prime Minister MacDonald also believes that Germany's unconditional return to the League of Nations is a matter that can be considered. Le Petit Parisien reported, "All countries that love peace must establish a barrier to prevent Germany from violating the treaty again, such as economic and financial sanctions." Le Matin reported, "A country that violates a treaty should be regarded as an aggressor. Japan Observes Development Quietly 26

However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has decided to take a quiet observation policy. In the recent situation, Japan and the United States are paying attention to East Asia and the Americas. As for the problems of Europe, they should also be resolved between the European countries. If the situation in Europe, taking advantage of the opportunity of the Stresa conference, is gradually returning to the dangerous state before the Great War, then countries outside Europe should not participate, and the problem should be limited to Europe. (Dentsu Telegram, 12th)

Belgium Does Not Allow Other Countries' Troops into its Territory; No Other Obligations Besides the Locarno Treaty; Minister of the Army Makes a Solemn Statement 28

Brussels – Belgian Minister of the Army De Visscher solemnly stated in the Chamber of Representatives that troops from other countries have absolutely no right to pass through Belgium, because Belgium has no other obligations besides the Locarno Pact. The Minister of the Army also said that Belgium has not concluded any other treaties besides the Pact, and the Locarno Pact has not been amended through diplomatic action. (National Telegram, 12th)

Italy Allocates Funds to Expand its Air Force, Aiming to Complete the Plan within Two Years 29

(Rome) The Official Gazette states that the Italian government has allocated 1.2 billion lire to improve and expand the air force. The funds will be allocated in three installments, with 600 million lire allocated this year, and then 300 million lire allocated each year thereafter. In this way, the Italian air force can complete its expansion plan from last year in the summer of 1937. (National Telegram, 12th)

Italian-Ethiopian Border Dispute: Italy is Willing to Arbitrate Through Negotiations According to the 1928 Treaty 30

(Geneva) The Ethiopian government sent a note to the Secretariat of the League of Nations on March 29 regarding the dispute between Italy and Ethiopia, stating that direct negotiations between Italy and Ethiopia had broken down and requesting that the matter be submitted to arbitration. Today, the Italian government telegraphed the Secretariat of the League of Nations, refuting the Ethiopian note, saying that direct negotiations between the governments of Italy and Ethiopia are still ongoing. The allegations in the Ethiopian note are mostly inaccurate or harbor ulterior motives. However, Italy does not want to argue to avoid causing unnecessary controversy. Furthermore, on January 19 of this year, Italy and Ethiopia exchanged notes, agreeing that disputes between the two countries would be submitted to conciliation or arbitration in accordance with the procedures stipulated in the Italian-Ethiopian treaty of August 2, 1928. However, after the Italian-Ethiopian treaty of 1928 was signed, the notes exchanged between the two countries stated that if a dispute arose that should be submitted to arbitration, then the governments of both countries should each appoint two arbitrators to arbitrate it. Therefore, the Italian government now intends to directly notify the Ethiopian government, expressing Italy's readiness to take the above-mentioned measures jointly with the Ethiopian government in order to achieve a final resolution to the dispute between the two countries. (Havas dispatch, 12th)

World Silver Price Could Stabilize in Months: Pittman's Speech to the U.S. Senate; Silver Movement in U.S. Congress Intensifies 31

(Washington) Democratic Senator Pittman stated in a Senate speech today that the Treasury's increase in domestic silver prices is solid evidence of the government's intention to implement the silver purchase law. Pittman, a leader of the silver faction and former U.S. representative who signed the London Silver Agreement, said today that the Treasury's action yesterday was President Roosevelt's response to those who generally believed he would not implement the silver purchase law. He also stated that, according to figures released by the Treasury, the President purchased 50 million ounces of silver each month, so there is no basis for criticizing the Treasury for saying that the government's silver purchases have slowed down. Pittman predicted that the world silver price could stabilize in a few months, and all problems could be resolved. It is believed here that the Treasury's increase in the domestic silver price from 64.5 cents to 71.11 cents is very important, as this move is indicative of the government's future monetary policy and the possibility of free coinage of silver. Some observers predict that when the silver price rises to $1.29 per ounce, free coinage of silver will be implemented, and the Treasury will not charge coinage taxes at that time. The leaders of the silver faction are still trying to raise the silver price. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has issued a warning, intending to prevent them from changing the current law through radical means. Morgenthau sent a letter to Democratic Senator McCarran, saying that if Congress disrupts the executive branch's power over gold and silver, the national currency system will be endangered. As for the source of Morgenthau's letter, it was because McCarran had proposed abolishing the provision in the silver purchase law that authorized the government to control or prohibit cash transactions and imports and exports. In addition, Senator Thomas, a leader of the silver faction in the Senate, also stated that although the silver faction was very pleased with the Treasury's increase in the silver price, they still intended to fight hard for Wheeler's proposal. Today, the Senate Agriculture Committee passed the bill, ordering the government to purchase 50 million ounces of silver per month until the silver price became sixteen to one against gold. The case was handled by the Agriculture Committee because its purpose was to relieve agriculture and livestock. In fact, it was also a tactic, as this would avoid being blocked by the more conservative Banking and Currency Committee. As for the content of the Wheeler Act, the Treasury must issue warehouse receipts for all the silver purchased. This expansionary proposal is opposed by the government. The Treasury announced this morning that in the past year, it has purchased 413,500,000 ounces of silver. As of March 27, the total amount of silver held by the Treasury was 1,104,500,000 ounces, while before the Silver Purchase Act was passed on May 25 last year, it was only 691,482,085 ounces. The Treasury estimates that the total value of all silver ingots and silver coins is $1,450,000,000, half of which was secretly purchased by the Treasury in the world silver market with a balance fund of $200 million. When the government nationalized silver last year, it obtained another 112,594,155 ounces, and the silver produced domestically reached 32,611,000 ounces. However, the Treasury still lacks 100 million ounces to achieve the goal of gold to silver reserves of three to one. (National Telegraph, 11th)

(Washington) Members of Congress are now closely watching the silver situation, wanting to see whether President Roosevelt's action of raising the Treasury's silver purchase price will curb or promote this movement. However, the silver movement is now flourishing again. The most prominent is Wheeler's silver coin bill, which advocates minting silver coins at a ratio of sixteen to one with gold. This bill was approved by the Senate Agriculture Committee today, but it is expected that the Senate will strongly oppose it. The actions of the committee and yesterday's developments have made the Congressional silver faction more active. Although the Senate leader is confident that the bill will not pass, the initiator, Wheeler, said that he will definitely get more votes of approval than before. Senator Pittman stated today that President Roosevelt's announcement has shown that he is eagerly fulfilling the terms of the London Silver Agreement and the Silver Purchase Act. Senator Tom has sent letters to prominent economists and financiers, predicting that countries still on the gold standard will soon abandon the gold standard, and then the world currency can be stabilized on a bimetallic basis. The more gold and silver the United States stores, the more dominant its position in controlling and stabilizing the world currency price will be. The world silver market is now rising in price. The New York large bar was listed at 65.75 cents, and then rose to 66 cents. Western mining is extremely happy due to increased subsidies. Public opinion generally believes that silver is mostly a by-product of mining. Before silver production increases, the price of other metals will inevitably increase. They predict that the future silver price will definitely be $1.29, but the final possible price depends on Washington's final decision and various factors, the main one being whether most of the silver hoarded in the Far East can be attracted to the market by a good price. According to currency experts, current developments do not have special inflationary properties, but if this procedure is actively carried out for a long period of time, there is a high possibility of inflation. They predict that the pressure from the Congressional silver faction to raise the silver price may not decrease until the silver price is close to $1.29. (Reuters, 11th)

(Washington) Some sources say that President Roosevelt raised the silver price as a preemptive defense, fearing that the silver faction would make more severe demands. However, Wall Street people do not believe this statement, saying that even if the Treasury is unwilling to fully implement the silver program, the silver faction has indeed succeeded in making the authorities pay attention to the terms of the silver purchase act. However, if the Treasury's gold reserves increase day by day, and the amount of silver reserves cannot increase at the same rate, then the silver program will not be possible to implement. According to news from the Treasury today, the monetary value of the silver stored by the Treasury, including large bar silver coins and silver coins in circulation, is $145 million. Therefore, to achieve a gold to silver ratio of three to one, it is necessary to purchase another $142.1 million in silver. According to the Treasury's recent report, the gold it holds is currently worth $861.4 million. (Reuters, 11th)

International Commercial Telegram - Special Business Report from Reuters on April 12th 80

Gold and Silver: London Gold Market - Trading was light, with the price at 144 shillings and 1 penny, half a penny higher than yesterday's closing price.

London Silver - Due to large-scale purchases by speculators and few sellers, the price of silver rose by 1.625 pence, reaching a new record since 1926. The spot price is 31.3125 pence, and the futures price is 31.4375 pence. The United States and China sold when prices rose. The morning session closed with uncertain sentiment.

Bombay Silver - The silver market was very volatile today, with prices rising and falling sharply throughout the day. Trading was very active. The spot price opened at 72 rupees and 5 annas at 10:00 AM, up 21 annas. It fell to 71 rupees and 14 annas an hour later, but returned to 72 rupees and 4 annas at noon and then stabilized. The closing price fell slightly again, so the latest price is 71 rupees and 15 annas, still 15 annas higher than yesterday's close.

Mount Riri Silver - The first transaction for September futures rose 245 pounds and was at 70.10. The July price was 68.30, 140 pounds higher than yesterday's close. The opening price for December was 71.00, 200 pounds higher.

Exchange Rates: British-American - The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The opening exchange rate between British and American currencies was 4 dollars and 85 cents, 25 points higher than yesterday's American-British close. Fluctuations were small before noon. The price was 4 dollars and 83 cents 625 points at 1:00 PM, and 4 dollars and 84 cents 125 points at 2:00 PM, 875 points lower than the opening price. However, transactions were scarce, and the market was calm.

Securities: New York - The New York stock market this morning paid the most attention to silver. Silver ore stocks soared, and various metal stocks also improved as a result. Other stocks were neglected. Overall, except for metal stocks, general market prices did not change much from yesterday's close. However, cotton mill stocks and rubber industry stocks were adversely affected by falling commodity prices.

A Record of Inspection in the Northwest: The Livelihood of the People in Longde and the Strategic Importance of Sanguankou 83

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya of this Newspaper

Leaving the eastern city of Jingning and winding through the Eastern Gorge, we arrived at Longde County, 38 kilometers away. The willows along the way, continuously in sight, were planted by Zuo Zongtang when he supervised Shaanxi twenty years ago. Commonly known as "Lord Zuo's Willows," they have a commemorative meaning. The trees are mostly more than one arm's length thick and two or three lengths tall, spaced three or four steps apart, forming rows along the road. In summer, the branches and leaves provide shade, benefiting travelers greatly. We passed forty or fifty refugees, men, women, old and young, hunching over, carrying and supporting each other, walking slowly on the muddy road. Upon inquiry, we learned that they were from Hejian and Xian County in Hebei Province. In recent years, the Hutuo River flooded, and the fields and houses were turned into a lake. They originally intended to go to the Northeast, but because it was difficult to leave the pass, they decided to go west to Jiayuguan to cultivate land and make a living. From their home to here, they have been walking for two months. The oldest is 68 years old, and the youngest is only four months old. They beg for food and assistance along the way, dividing it equally according to shares. Those over ten years old get a full share, and those under nine get half a share. They have the ancient tradition of sharing joys and sorrows and are as close as family. However, carrying the old and leading the young, they travel only twenty or thirty miles a day. Reaching their destination may be after the rainy season.

The city of Longde is backed by high mountains and is large and difficult to defend. From 1926 to 1931, bandits captured the city eleven times. The city walls collapsed, and the people's houses were desolate. Whenever there is a disturbance, few soldiers cannot defend it, and many soldiers cannot be supported. Relying on the city is also unreliable. The entire county covers about 9,000 square miles, divided into twenty-one forts, with a population of about 60,000. The annual miscellaneous silver is more than 3,400 yuan, and the grain is more than 700 dan. There are two higher primary schools, one with more than 160 students and one with more than 220 students. There is one model elementary school with 70+ students. There are twenty-six village elementary schools, totaling less than 300 students. Students have no cotton clothes in winter and must help with farm work in summer. In reality, the number of students attending class often differs from the enrollment. Teachers' annual salaries of 20 yuan are also quite meager. The people's livelihood is such that they commonly cook thin yellow millet porridge with the husks on, and stir-fried noodles made from oats and wheat. The price of goods is such that one yuan can buy two dou of yellow millet, or three dou of naked oats, three dou and five sheng of oats (each dou of wheat weighs 30 catties), six and a half catties of meat, and eight or nine catties of salt. Although it is said to be not expensive, they cannot afford it. About two-thirds of the people still wear single pants in winter. Many children of several years old are especially naked without pants, and babies are even held in their clothes. The clothes are tattered, and the babies' purple and red frozen legs are often exposed. In the night, it is difficult to find one family out of a hundred with bedding. Most people huddle around the stove and sleep on the kang (brick bed) to get through the night. I once asked several farmers if they had cotton quilts for warmth. One replied, "We don't even have chopsticks, how can we have quilts?" The words were sorrowful, and nothing could be more so. However, the reason why the farmers are so poor is not because they are lazy or the land is barren, but because military requisitions and miscellaneous taxes are too heavy, and they have already been completely exploited. For example, in the neighboring county of Gangu, there was no rain all year round last year, but the allocated requisitions still reached 200,000 yuan. With the amount exceeding the allocation for four years in one year, how can the farmers bear it? It is found that in the Qing Dynasty, Gansu relied entirely on subsidies from various provinces. Since the subsidies were cut off, the income and expenditure were far from sufficient. Those in charge of accounting and administration could not cope, so they used the requisition system for turnover. The authorities once considered abolishing the requisition system to unify finances, but due to the special circumstances, it has not been resolved. Moreover, the financial difficulties of the provinces are actually due to the excessive inter-provincial support of military expenditures. The heavy military expenditures in recent years, especially in eastern Gansu, often led to spending tomorrow's grain today, so that the requisitions in each county exceeded the allocated amount. If this trend continues, it will inevitably follow the example of Sichuan Province.

I stayed overnight in Longde. The next morning, I departed east and arrived at Yangjia Shop, 9 kilometers away, at the foot of Liupan Mountain. From here, I climbed up the mountain in twists and turns, with more than a dozen turns. The power lines run straight up the winding road. Although there are high poles to support them, the power lines are so low and sloped that they almost touch the mountain surface. The steepness of the mountain slope can be imagined. It took seven or eight kilometers (commonly known as fifteen li each up and down) to reach the top of the mountain. The grass is vigorous, the stone layers are scarlet, and the peaks are surrounded like stars surrounding the throne. However, the clouds and mist in the valley bottom make it impossible to look down. Han Qi of the Song Dynasty defeated Yuan Wu of the Western Xia Dynasty here. Emperor Genghis Khan of the Yuan Dynasty repeatedly avoided the summer heat on Liupan Mountain and is said to have died here on his way back west. He is buried in the mountain, and there is still a tomb without a stele in the territory of Guyuan. Descending the eastern foothills, the slopes wind left and right for more than twenty turns, six or seven kilometers long. Halfway up the mountain is a Guandi Temple, but there is no forest scenery at all. Lord Zuo's willows are planted on the west side and in the middle of the mountain, while on the east side, they end at the foot of the mountain. Down the mountain is a village called Monk Shop, the former site of He Shang Yuan, which was guarded by the Song envoy Wu Jie. A clear stream flows beside the village, which is one of the sources of the Jing River. The road follows the stream, and six kilometers to the Wating Post. When Kui Xiao of the Han Dynasty heard that Luoyang had fallen, he sent Niu Han to guard this place. He also set up a stronghold here when he came, named Wating Pass. The castle is towering and has a commanding position. From here, Lord Zuo's willows stretch continuously. The porcelain bowls of the power lines are occasionally nailed to them, which is very convenient. The water flow gradually increases, and the mountain cliffs on both banks are steep, dangerous, and strangely shaped. About eight or nine kilometers away, two peaks face each other, with a line running through the middle. The cliffs flank the water, which is about ten feet wide. The rushing torrents are abundant and heroic. A stone bridge is inscribed with the words "Second Pass," also known as Jinfo Gorge. There is a Guandi Temple beside the mountain, and there is also a statue of Yang Yanzhao, commonly known as the Sixth Son Temple. A few steps east of the bridge, there are three or four houses, and there is a "Former Residence of Dong Shao Bao" stele. After ascending a gentle slope, we arrived at HaoDian Town. From Wating to the town, the canyon is eleven and a half kilometers long. In ancient times, it was Danzheng Gorge. During the Tang Dynasty, it was the boundary with Tubo. Its importance for offense and defense can be imagined. East of Liupan Mountain, dozens of wild pheasants can be seen in groups, lying on the ground facing the sun. They are not startled by passing vehicles. HaoDian Town has more than a hundred residents. Seeing the Guyuan branch card of the Anti-Opium Rehabilitation Bureau, I knew that it was not the territory of Pingliang. Sixteen kilometers to Pingliang County City. The streets are wide and tidy, and the city is crowded, making it a large county in eastern Gansu. The inn where I stayed overnight was also more satisfactory than the previous stations, which did not even have doors and windows.

The Garrison Headquarters Orders to Enlist and Pacify People in Three Provinces to Return to Farming, Considering Preservation, Nourishment and Education. The Expeditionary Forces Against Bandits in Sichuan and Guizhou Have Repeatedly Captured Famous Cities. 84

Correspondence from Hankou: The border area of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei and Anhui has been plagued by banditry for a long time, and the people have been displaced. Now that the bandits have been suppressed, but the people have not been settled, and the land lies barren, without anyone to cultivate it. The Garrison Headquarters of the Military Committee has repeatedly received reports from various parties, fearing that the spring plowing will be delayed and the people will become more displaced. The government of the three provinces has been strictly ordered to instruct the administrative heads of the border areas to properly enlist and pacify people to return to farming, and to consider the three aspects of preservation, nourishment and education. The order said, "It has been found that the border area of Henan, Hubei and Anhui has been plagued by bandits for a long time, with fields and gardens lying barren and houses in ruins. Since our army's advance to suppress them, the major bandit gangs have been suppressed, but the people in various places have either been threatened by the bandits and scattered to other places, or fear that the bandits will return after the troops leave, suffering another catastrophe, or are unable to move forward due to lack of food and clothing. As a result, only the old and weak remain in the recovered bandit areas, and the displaced people are everywhere, with no way to settle them. Thinking of the future, I cannot help but feel deeply saddened. The Garrison Headquarters has repeatedly received reports from various parties that the counties in the border area are devastated, with no one to cultivate the land and a famine looming. With spring plowing imminent, if preparations are not made early, how can we revitalize the countryside and pacify the people? Now that the major bandit gangs have been wiped out, there is no need to worry about the remnant bandits. In addition to ordering the garrison troops in the border area to thoroughly suppress the remnant bandits in conjunction with the military and civilians in accordance with the "Spiritual Transformation Plan for the Military and Civilians" promulgated by the former Nanchang Garrison Headquarters, the provincial governments should be ordered to immediately follow the "Plan for Reorganizing the Baojia and Suppressing Remnant Bandits in the Bandit Areas" and refer to the regulations of Jiangxi for revising and recruiting the displaced people in various counties, strictly instructing the administrative heads of the border areas to earnestly handle the matter. How to inform the people to return to farming, organize the people to defend themselves, settle the people to enjoy their work, support the people to produce, and guide the people to be virtuous, should all be carefully discussed and properly implemented, so as to consider the three aspects of preservation, nourishment and education, so that spring plowing will not be delayed and the people will not be displaced. This is of utmost importance."

In recent days, news of the military expedition against bandits in Sichuan and Guizhou has been frequently heard and has been very smooth. Xu bandits of Northern Sichuan are now in the area west of the Jialing River, engaged in fierce fighting with Deng Xihou's troops. Deng's troops won victories in the battles of Sanlei Dam and the upper reaches of the Baihe River at Chaba Meizi Dam, Guanyin Hall, Ganxi River, Phoenix Mountain, Maming Temple, Maling Temple, and Wushu Post. They are now in contact with Hu Zongnan's division to jointly block and suppress the bandits. The Fifth Route Army has recovered the two cities of Nanjiang and Tongjiang. The Third and Fourth Route Armies have also been ordered to sweep across the eastern bank of the Jialing River. There are currently no traces of bandits, and the remnant forces of Xu bandits are surrounded and can be expected to be eliminated. The Guizhou bandits who crossed the Wujiang River were also defeated by the National Army. According to Li Shizeng, who passed through Hankou the day before, the situation in that area is very smooth due to President Chiang's stationing and supervision. Chiang is determined to eliminate the remnant bandits and will not leave until the military affairs have come to an end. (11th)

Thirty-Three Counties in Jiangxi Have Been Lifted From Blockade, and the Provincial Government Has Issued an Order to Restore Free Trade. 85

Correspondence from Nanchang: The blockade of various places in Jiangxi Province has been in effect for several years. The circulation and purchase of oil, salt, kerosene, and daily necessities have all been subject to unified control and restrictions. At this moment the bandits in various places have been put down gradually. Apart from new recovery areas and areas connected to new recovery areas, and remote complex regions where there are still remaining bandits that are yet to be pacified, the inland area has been entirely cleared up. The provincial government recently followed the orders of the Garrison Headquarters and lifted the blockade on thirty-three counties, including Jiujiang, Linchuan, Dongxiang, and Jinxian, restoring free trade. Previous public sales and salt purchase tickets have been abolished. However, salt shipments of more than 100 catties still require the issuance of mystery permits by the local government to prevent them from flowing into neighboring bandit areas, so as to show strict enforcement. The regions that have not been pacified will continue to tighten the blockade, such as Yudu, Huichang, Dexing, Hengfeng, Tonggu and other counties, where oil and salt are still sold publicly. (April 10th)

Japanese Consuls in Xiamen and Fuzhou Crack Down on Illegal Activities by Taiwanese Residents, Limiting the Time for Gambling Dens to Close and Requiring Registration of Weapons 86

Correspondence from Xiamen: Since November, Japan's policy towards Fujian has undergone some changes. The most obvious example is the crackdown by the Japanese consuls in Xiamen and Fuzhou on illegal activities by Taiwanese people. Previously, after the commander of the Third Fleet of the Japanese Foreign Dispatch Fleet, Hyakutake Gengo, visited Xiamen, the Japanese consul in Xiamen, Tsukamoto Takeshi, issued two orders: (1) Crack down on gambling dens set up by Taiwanese people in Xiamen, requiring them to close down completely by the end of April. From May 1st onwards, Taiwanese people are not allowed to operate any gambling dens. (2) Crack down on the possession of weapons by Taiwanese people, ordering them to register all weapons at the Japanese consulate for inspection before March 15th. At the same time, those carrying guns are required to register with the Xiamen Public Security Bureau. (3) Taiwanese people are not allowed to operate small pawnshops without the permission of the Japanese consulate or to receive any mortgages. The gambling dens have gradually been closed down in accordance with the order, but the result will be that several thousand Taiwanese vagrants who make a living in the gambling dens will lose their jobs. Someone suggested that after the gambling dens are closed, the four major clubs, namely the Paper Weaving and Four Major Clubs, should accommodate the unemployed Taiwanese people. The Japanese consul has not yet allowed it. The Japanese consulate has already implemented the registration of firearms, and the Public Security Bureau has also issued a notice limiting the time for registration. As for opium dens, since the Anti-Opium Bureau already has regulations, they only need to comply with them, so there is no order to close them down. In addition, regarding the investigation of bandits, in the past, it was necessary to conduct searches of Taiwanese residences in conjunction with Japanese police. Recently, due to the Haihou Maoji robbery case, the Public Security Bureau can directly execute searches of foreign firms and arrest Taiwanese people before extraditing them. These are the recent developments of the Japanese in Xiamen. In Fuzhou, the Japanese consul, Usami, has also recently taken similar steps to Xiamen. At the end of March, he ordered the Taiwanese Association of Fuzhou to instruct the gambling dens opened by Taiwanese people to close down completely from April 1st. Opium dens should follow the regulations promulgated by the Chinese authorities and obtain licenses from the Anti-Opium Bureau. The Taiwanese people also requested permission to keep four gambling dens, specializing in Pai Gow and Fan Tan, to make a living, but the Japanese consul did not allow it. April 1st was the date for the implementation of the closure. The Japanese consul specially dispatched Japanese police to inspect the gambling dens to see if they were complying with the order to close down. However, it is said that they have indeed stopped during the day, but there is still a lot of gambling at night. In Fuzhou and Xiamen, there are fewer Taiwanese people in Fuzhou than in Xiamen, only a few thousand, and their residence is limited to the Cangshan area, so it is easier to crack down. In Xiamen, there are many Taiwanese people, about 20,000, and they are scattered in various streets and lanes throughout the city, so it is more difficult to crack down. Although the Japanese consuls in Fuzhou and Xiamen have made this statement, the actual result of the implementation is still unpredictable. (April 8th)

Fujian Province: Agricultural Relief Plan to be Handled with the Assistance of the Farmers Bank 87

Fuzhou Correspondence: Previously, in order to provide relief to the rural villages in the counties that were afflicted by the bandits, the Fujian Provincial Government especially established the Rural Finance Relief Office. It collaborated with the Fuzhou branch of the Chinese Farmers Bank, and the relief office dispatched personnel to various counties to establish loan offices, guide farmers in various villages to organize mutual aid societies, and borrow money from the loan offices to lend to the members to buy farm implements, seeds, and fertilizer. The money released by the loan offices was borrowed from the Farmers Bank by the Relief Office. Since the implementation of the plan, it has had remarkable results. A total of 52 mutual aid societies were established in Minhou County, with loans of 20,000 yuan. In Fuqing County, 63 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 20,000 yuan. In Shaowu County, 68 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 15,000 yuan. In Changle County, 45 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 15,000 yuan. In Chong'an County, 32 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 10,000 yuan. In Shunchang County, 50 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 10,000 yuan. In Pucheng County, 38 mutual aid societies were established, with loans of 10,000 yuan. The total amount of loans issued has reached 100,000 yuan. Now that the spring plowing is beginning, the farmers are in urgent need of money, and the amount of loans released by the Farmers Bank has been exhausted. Last month, the director of the Relief Office, Mr. Huo, and the manager of the branch, Mr. Shen, went to Hankou together to contact the head office for an increase in the loan amount and to promote the rural farmers' relief efforts. As a result, they were quite successful. It is now reported that the head office has agreed to expand the Fuzhou branch into a branch office, in order to raise its status and assist the pawn industry. A farmers' pledge office will be established, specializing in financial turnover institutions for farmers. Objects will be pledged at the lowest interest rate. At the same time, it will cooperate with the government to establish agricultural warehouses, allowing farmers to deposit grain in the warehouses after the harvest and redeem it at the original price when there is a shortage of grain. The above-mentioned aspects of rural economic relief are all passive aspects. The active aspects of improving farmers' technology and developing agricultural production are the responsibility of the Construction Bureau. The Construction Bureau is planning to establish a provincial agricultural test site in Quanzhou, and an electric irrigation bureau in Changle. The construction has already begun, and Xinghua has been designated as a sugar industry revival test area. A loan of 100,000 yuan has been obtained from the banking group to improve the variety of sugar cane and sugar production. A tea research institute will be established in Sandu to guide tea farmers in Fuding to improve tea planting and tea production. Meteorological observation stations will be established in Nanping, Pucheng, and Changting to be used for agricultural purposes. The Education Department will be consulted to move the provincial Fuzhou Advanced Agricultural School to Zhangzhou, the agricultural center of southern Fujian, in order to adapt to the environment and seek development. (April 10th)

The New Life Movement Promotion Association Issues the Organizational Outline of the Labor Service Corps and the Preliminary Implementation Plan for the "Three Transformations" of Life 88

Correspondence from Nanchang: The New Life Movement Promotion Association recently issued a notice to the New Life Movement Promotion Associations in various places, attaching the "Organizational Outline of the New Life Labor Service Corps" and the "Preliminary Implementation Plan for the Militarization, Industrialization, and Artification of Life." The original text is recorded as follows:

Announcement 89

Since its inception last year, the New Life Movement has primarily focused on "order" and "cleanliness" as the central tasks of its first phase. Fortunately, with the concerted efforts and enthusiastic promotion of various dignitaries and compatriots nationwide, the perception of this movement and the awareness of "order" and "cleanliness" have deeply penetrated people's hearts, gradually becoming a prevailing trend. With a solid foundation established, progress is promising. Future work should not only maintain and enrich past achievements but also further promote advancement. Now, to adapt to the needs of our nation and develop the vitality of our people, to realize the three major principles of militarization, productionization, and artification as outlined in the New Life Movement's guidelines within the daily lives of all compatriots nationwide, and to achieve the rationalization of national life, we have specially formulated preliminary implementation plans for the militarization, productionization, and artification of life. All kinds of New Life Movement work activity groups are uniformly reorganized into labor service corps. The central goal of this year's New Life Movement is to promote various tasks in the three-pronged plan with the spirit of labor service. The main tasks include: (1) implementing public training and organization, (2) promoting the organization of social cooperative enterprises, and (3) intensifying the popularization of various social educations. The organization of labor service corps should be based on public officials, school teachers and students, and leaders of various industries. They should engage in work utilizing spare time after official duties, classes, work, or during other holidays. Our association will formulate organizational outlines and send them out together with the preliminary implementation plan of the three-pronged approach. It is hoped that you will refer to and consider the local conditions, properly draft implementation plans and detailed implementation plans, as well as various organizational rules for the labor service corps, and submit them to the association for review. The overall goal is to be thorough, detailed, and practical for implementation, and then gradually promote them, so that this central movement can deeply penetrate the people, achieve remarkable results, and solidify the foundation of the country with the development of the New Life Movement. The future of the nation truly depends on it. President Chiang Kai-shek.

Organizational Outline of the New Life Labor Service Corps 90

In recent years, our country has experienced natural disasters and man-made calamities, internal troubles and foreign invasions. Poverty and crises have reached an extreme. Everything is waiting to be revived, but cannot be revived. Everything is waiting to be started, but cannot be started. The reason is due to the declining national spirit, the dispirited morale, the love of ease and aversion to work, the greed for food and laziness, harming others for personal gain, abusing public office for private benefit, and a lack of the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation. Those who can respect public morals, pay attention to group life, strive and sacrifice for the nation, and diligently serve the society and the people are rare. As a result, the 400 million people have become a pile of loose sand and have completely lost the power of independence and autonomy. All nations in the world today take the entire strength as the unit of competition for survival. However, our nation alone is living in a drunken dream and sleeping soundly in selfish individualism. How can we not be sacrificed by the power of the times? If we want to change the atmosphere and revive the nation as a plan to save the country and ourselves, we can only awaken the people, take labor as our duty, take service as our purpose, not spare our own sweat and blood, support our own country, not fear difficulties and dangers, not be afraid of hard work, and then organize the people, promote education, relieve unemployment, increase production, support the people's morale, transform society, and promote various constructions, in order to create the foundation of modern national obligatory labor. In order to realize the labor service movement, our association plans to uniformly reorganize all kinds of New Life Movement work activity groups into labor service corps. The military police, service personnel of party, government, and military agencies, school teachers and students, social groups, and leaders of various industries, based on the spirit of labor service, promote the three plans of militarization, productionization, and artification of life. Responsible personnel should be responsible for the organization, ensuring that the personnel under their command serve the society for one hour of labor service every day. The persons in charge of the New Life Movement in various places should especially follow the purpose of setting an example in person, engage in leadership, create a trend, make everyone regard labor service as valuable, and make them know that labor is the duty of life and service is the natural vocation of life. Then, together and unanimously, we will cooperate and unite into the entire strength of the nation to jointly devote ourselves to the great cause of national rejuvenation. The new life of our Republic of China lies in this. We specially formulate the outline as follows:

(1) In order to increase the efficiency of the New Life Movement, our association takes labor service as the center and promotes the "Preliminary Implementation Plan for the Militarization, Productionization, and Artification of Life," and organizes various labor service corps separately.

(2) The military police, faculty and students, party, government, and military agencies, various service personnel, women, and various social groups in various places may, in accordance with this outline and considering the local conditions, separately formulate simple organizational rules and establish labor service corps.

(3) Various labor service corps are organized by local or institutional groups. Their names may be determined according to the nature of the respective constituent elements and the names of the institutions. For example, "Nanchang City Women's New Life Labor Service Corps" "Pinghan Railway Employees' New Life Labor Service Corps," etc.

(4) Various labor service corps are directly subordinate to and guided by the local New Life Movement Promotion Association.

(5) Various labor service corps shall set up one director and one deputy director, who shall be filled by the responsible personnel of the constituent agencies or groups, or appointed by the local New Life Movement Association, or elected by the members. The group may be divided into teams and groups below the team, each team and group shall be set up a captain and a leader, which shall be appointed by the team leader. The detailed organization shall be the responsibility of the New Life Movement members in various places to formulate and implement themselves.

(6) The work of the labor service corps should be promoted separately in accordance with the "Preliminary Implementation Plan for the Militarization, Productionization, and Artification of Life" formulated by the General Association. In order to facilitate implementation, special regulations are made on the promotion plan as follows: 1. Punctuality Movement, 2. Public Literacy Movement, 3. Work-Study Movement (such as selling newspapers, selling books, writing letters, etc.) 4. Physical Exercise, 5. Group Education, 6. Social Hygiene Movement, 7. Promoting Cooperative Movement, 8. Promoting Baojia Movement, 9. Utilizing Waste Material Campaign, 10. Assisting in Household Investigation Campaign, 11. Assisting Police Investigation Campaign, 12. Canal Digging and Embankment Construction Movement, 13. Bridge Repair and Road Repair Movement, 14. Afforestation and Forest Collection Movement, 15. Promoting Savings and Insurance Movement, 16. Promoting the Use of Domestic Goods Movement, 17. Aiding the Old, Weak, Disabled, and Injured Movement, 18. Maintaining Decency and Aiding Those in Danger Movement, 19. Smoking and Gambling Cessation Movement, 20. Aviation and Air Defense Movement, 21. Promoting Scientific Movement.

(7) Each labor service corps may also select the work that is similar to its own nature from the various movements listed in the previous article and implement it in a practical way. They may also set a certain movement according to the season as the central work of each season (such as planting trees in spring, hygiene in summer, cooperation in autumn, road construction and relief in winter, etc.). The specific implementation plan and steps shall be drafted by the New Life Movement in various places and submitted for approval.

(8) Each member of the labor service corps must use their spare time after official duties, classes, and work to carry out labor service for at least one hour every day.

(9) Members of the labor service corps should receive training and obey the discipline of the group. The training methods and the discipline to be observed shall be stipulated by the General Association.

(10) The work situation of each labor service corps should be reported to the New Life Movement Promotion Association where it is located on a monthly basis.

(11) After the establishment of various labor service corps in various places, report to the local New Life Movement Promotion Association and forward it to our association for record. (To be continued)

Wuxi: Deed Tax Reduction Deadline at the End of the Month 91

The county government announced that the deed tax rate for fields and houses in this province was originally 9.6%, but was reduced to 6.3% from May of the 23rd year. Initially, the limit was three months, but it was extended twice for three months each time. It will expire at the end of January this year. After deliberation by the 717th meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, it was decided to extend the deadline for another three months due to the impact of last year's drought, which will end at the end of April. Those who continue to wait and see and conceal information will be mistaken. Once the extension expires, the collection will be strictly enforced. At that time, not only will the tax rate increase, but the penalties will also be heavier. A notice was issued yesterday, requiring all recent deeds and old deeds that have not been taxed to be taxed in full before the deadline at the end of April. District chiefs, township chiefs, and town chiefs should publicize this widely at any time and earnestly supervise and urge the payment.

Relief Committee Distributes Spring Relief 92

The Wuxi County Relief Committee is handling spring relief in this county. It was previously decided that, due to the extremely wide disaster area and the odd shortage of donations, the relief will only be distributed in the old Huaishang and Tianxia markets in the fifth and seventh districts, which are the most severely affected disaster areas. It was entrusted to district chiefs Zhao Hongbin and Du Xizhen for thorough investigation. As a result, there are more than 5,500 households in various townships in Huaishang and more than 2,500 households in Tianxia, totaling more than 8,000 households. It has now been decided to distribute 2.5 pecks of white rice per household, totaling more than 2,000 stones of rice. The foreign rice has also been purchased and the passport has been obtained in Shanghai. Zhao Du, the two district chiefs and township chief Jiang Ousun, etc., were notified by telegram yesterday to conduct a consultation, and the rice will be transported to the rural areas and distributed to households immediately.

Yan Chengqi, the patrol captain of the Public Security Bureau in Hetangqiao, District 5, went to the countryside to arrest soil dealer Ge Lao Si and others a few days ago. Changzhou: Wujiao Road Construction Survey 94

In order to facilitate traffic in Jiaoxi Town in Wuyi County and prosper the markets along the road, the Wuyi County Government is building the Wujiao Road. Wang Baosu and others organized a long-distance bus company, submitted an application for a contract, and obtained approval from the Construction Department for the record. The road is 25 kilometers long and the measurement project is expected to be completed in one week. If the road construction project progresses smoothly, it can start within days.

Zhenjiang: Special Commissioners for Handling Opium Cases Set Up in Various Counties 95

The Provincial Anti-Smoking Association previously stipulated that counties that do not concurrently handle judicial affairs should set up special commissioners for handling opium cases, with the responsibility assigned to them. The method is for each county to select several people and submit them to the Provincial Association for qualification review and appointment. More than a dozen counties have already started reporting. In addition, the plan for the Crafts Institute for Opium Addicts, which the association is planning to set up in Nantong, has been drafted. The location is in Xiaohai Town, Nantong, with a budget of 15,000 yuan, which will be shared equally by the province and county.

Ningbo: Carelessness in Songfu Hospital 97

Songfu Hospital at No. 59, Zhenming Road, Yongbu was founded by Rong Songfu from Cixi and has been in operation for more than ten years. The hospital building is a rented civilian house, with two courtyards in the front and back, a total of three buildings with upper story and three single-story buildings. Rong Songfu's wife, Ms. Feng, and her three daughters lived in the hospital. Recently, Songfu went to Shanghai for business, and his wife, Ms. Feng, went to the Daguangming Theater in Xinjie to watch a play with her daughters after dinner yesterday evening. Only the maid was left in the hospital to take care of it. Unexpectedly, around 11 o'clock, a fire suddenly broke out in the hospital. It took half an hour to put it out. All six hospital buildings were destroyed, and the loss was quite huge.

Letter 99

Dear Editor,

I am writing to you regarding the news item "Fire at Hangzhou Salt Affairs Audit Office" published on the local edition of your newspaper on April 9, which mentioned that the fire was caused by carelessness due to electrical leakage. After investigation by personnel dispatched by our factory, it was found that the electrical lighting equipment in the guard room that was burned in the fire was repaired last year, and there should be no electrical leakage. Before the true cause of the fire is found, it is difficult to make a guess. The report that the fire was caused by electrical leakage may be because the guards intended to shirk responsibility, so they made this excuse. After the dispatched personnel inspected the fire scene, there were only burnt pillars and tiles left, and the electrical wires had also been burned into black copper, making it impossible to prove that it was caused by electrical leakage. The details are written to you in a letter for correction. Please publish the truth to clarify the truth.

Sincerely,

Hangzhou Electric Power Co., Ltd.

April 10,

Chairman's Report: After the rituals, Chairman Jiang Huaisu first reported, saying that the General of our Party led the revolution and had a policy of accommodating the communists in the 13th year of the Republic of China. At that time, many revolutionaries were anesthetized by the Communist Party and joined the Communist Party. Among them, there were many who had ability. The General admitted communist members to participate in the National Revolution in order to make these able young people re-enter the right path. With the General's great personality, they were taught the Three People's Principles of the great revolution, knowing that they would definitely realize it and work hard for the Kuomintang. In recent years, all kinds of unprecedented cruel behaviors have caused China to suffer unprecedented catastrophes. Now that the Red Bandits have reached the end of their rope, we should unify our thoughts, unify our will, and show great strength. The National Revolution will definitely succeed one day.

Credit Loans Should Be Discussed with the Three Banks: Ministry of Finance's Reply to the Chamber of Commerce, etc. 104

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, local associations, previously drafted a four-point outline for handling small industrial and commercial credit loans to revive the market. They submitted it to the Ministry of Finance, requesting an allocation of 2.5 million yuan to form a syndicate with the financial community to handle the loans. The Ministry of Finance replied to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating: We have received your submission. The situation of industry and commerce in Shanghai does indeed necessitate relief. We previously received your association's petition for relief, which has already been approved. Now, regarding the outline for handling small industrial and commercial credit loans you submitted, specifically the third item stipulating that the government would allocate 2.5 million yuan, and the Shanghai Banking Association's statement that they had discussed and agreed to raise funds for small loans, the Ministry, considering the overall situation, and to consolidate finance and facilitate the relief of industry and commerce, has already implemented measures to increase bank capital and strengthen their financial power. All loan matters have been delegated to the banks. The Ministry, as an administrative organ, cannot directly lend money. We have instructed the Shanghai Banking Association to directly discuss specific measures with the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications (the "Three Banks"), and to implement loan disbursement according to banking regulations to provide relief. We have also sent separate letters of instruction. This is hereby notified. The Banking Association also received an instruction from the Ministry of Finance, Document No. 12703, stating: Regarding the Shanghai Local Association's resolution on the second article of the outline for handling small industrial and commercial credit loans, which stipulates that the government and the banking industry share the recognition of the total loan amount, please advise whether the Ministry should guide and form a syndicate with the banking industry, or devise other methods. We have received your submission, along with the submission from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association regarding the same matter. The situation of industry and commerce in Shanghai does indeed necessitate relief. The Ministry, considering the overall situation, and to consolidate finance and facilitate the relief of industry and commerce, has already implemented measures to increase bank capital and strengthen their financial power. All loan matters have been delegated to the banks. The Ministry, as an administrative organ, cannot directly lend money. We have sent separate letters to the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, instructing them to directly discuss specific measures with the association, and to implement loan disbursement according to banking regulations to provide relief. In addition to the instructions issued, you are hereby ordered to comply and report accordingly.

The Three Banks Obey Orders to Handle Loans: The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications have received orders from the Ministry of Finance to implement loan disbursement according to banking regulations to provide relief to industry and commerce. It is reported that all three banks have decided to adopt the same method as last year's year-end account settlement, specifically setting aside a large sum of money for interbank lending, to facilitate adjustment and indirectly relieve industry and commerce. Banks and money shops that apply can handle it according to the method used during last year's year-end account settlement. At the same time, they will consult with the Banking Association to discuss specific measures.

The Subcommittee Will Meet: The subcommittee organized by the Banking Association for small industrial and commercial credit loans, after raising 2.5 million yuan from member banks, originally planned to form a syndicate with the Central Bank after the Ministry of Finance allocated 2.5 million yuan. After the Ministry stated that it could not directly provide loans, it was decided to convene a meeting after Committee member Chen Guangfu returned to Shanghai from Beijing to discuss whether to form a syndicate solely by the banking industry, or to contact the Three Banks to discuss specific measures before making a decision. This will be put forward for discussion.
